      <script>
       // load jackpot banner
    $.get( "http://www.stanleybet.hr/inc/banner_jackpot.php", function( data ) {
    	$( ".jackpot" ).html( data );
    });

    // call jackpot banner
    var jackpot_call = function() {
      $.ajax({
      	type: "POST",
      	url: "http://www.stanleybet.hr/inc/banner_jackpot.php",
      	data: { jackpot_1: "10472.42", jackpot_2: "03275.11", jackpot_3: "00282.60", jackpot_4: "00000.00", jackpot_5: "00000.00", club_id: "1"}
      })
      .done(function( html ) {
      	$( ".jackpot" ).html( html );
      });
    };

    jackpot_call();

	// call every minute
	setInterval(function() {
		jackpot_call();
	}, 1000 * 60 * 1);
      </script>
